[0m[1m	          <div class="date-outer">\n
[0m[1m	        \n
[0m[1m	<h2 class='date-header'><span>Saturday, June 07, 2014</span></h2>\n
[0m[1m	\n
[0m[1m	          <div class="date-posts">\n
[0m[1m	        \n
[0m[1m	<div class='post-outer'>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http:[0m[1m//schema.org/BlogPosting'>\n
[0m[1m	<meta content='17476693' itemprop='blogId'/>\n
[0m[1m	<meta content='743955863121505681' itemprop='postId'/>\n
[0m[1m	<a name='743955863121505681'></a>\n
[0m[1m	<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<a href='http:[0m[1m//blacknwhitemovement.blogspot.com/2014/06/ang-puno-ng-manggang-hitik-sa-pamumunga.html'>ANG PUNO NG MANGGANG HITIK SA PAMUMUNGA... PINUPUKOL</a>\n
[0m[1m	</h3>\n
[0m[1m	<div class='post-header'>\n
[0m[1m	<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>\n
[0m[1m	</div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-743955863121505681' itemprop='description articleBody'>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom:[0m[1m .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;">\n
[0m[1m[32m	<span style="font-family:[0m[1m &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">By Raul Socrates Banzuela</span></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom:[0m[1m .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;">\n
[0m[1m[32m	<span style="font-family:[0m[1m &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;"><br /></span></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom:[0m[1m .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;">\n
[0m[1m[32m	<span style="font-family:[0m[1m &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">Ang puno ng manggang hitik sa\n
[0m[1m[32m	pamumunga...pinupukol.<o:[0m[1mp></o:p></span></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom:[0m[1m .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom:[0m[1m .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;">\n
[0m[1m[32m	<span style="font-family:[0m[1m &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">During the Langkaan Controversy in\n
[0m[1m	1990, the peasant movement was deeply united to defend Butch when he was being\n
[0m[1m	bypassed each time by the powerful Committee on ConfIrmation of Congress.\n
[0m[1m	&nbsp;The public debate then was raging whether or not the piece of prime\n
[0m[1m	agricultural land (Langkaan) in Cavite should give way to Joe Concepcion-supported\n
[0m[1m[32m	Marubeni industry.<o:[0m[1mp></o:p></span></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom:[0m[1m .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom:[0m[1m .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;">\n
[0m[1m[32m	<span style="font-family:[0m[1m &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">Having been among the staunch\n
[0m[1m	proponents of HB 400, which later became the Comprehensive Agrarian Reform Law\n
[0m[1m	(CARL), together with Edcel Lagman and the late Boni Gillego, Butch becoming\n
[0m[1m	Secretary of the DAR after the coup of 1989 and the ouster of Miriam as DAR\n
[0m[1m	Secretary, was received by the peasant and the NGO movement with great\n
[0m[1m	enthusiasm and anticipation of great things to come in the agrarian reform\n
[0m[1m	front. &nbsp;It was no surprise then that even Jimmy Tadeo of KMP who REJECTED\n
[0m[1m	CARP, came to join us in the gallery in the Senate supporting Butch's\n
[0m[1m	confirmation and to witness the gallant defense for Butch's confirmation by\n
[0m[1m[32m	some Senators like Nene Pimentel.&nbsp;<o:[0m[1mp></o:p></span></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom:[0m[1m .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom:[0m[1m .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;">\n
[0m[1m[32m	<span style="font-family:[0m[1m &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">The rest was history...and tragedy.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom:[0m[1m .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom:[0m[1m .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;">\n
[0m[1m[32m	<span style="font-family:[0m[1m &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">After a series of bypass, and an\n
[0m[1m	expected awkward situation in the Cabinet where Joe Concepcion, DTI Secretary,\n
[0m[1m	and Butch Abad, DAR Secretary, would be sitting side by side with President\n
[0m[1m	Cory, he finally succumbed and resigned. &nbsp;It was among the saddest moments\n
[0m[1m	in the peasant movement, feeling a great loss amidst the advance of&nbsp;the\n
[0m[1m	anti-reform forces.&nbsp; Twenty four years\n
[0m[1m	hence, almost all prime agricultural lands in CALABARZON has been wiped out, prime\n
[0m[1m	and precious limited alluvial soil cemented to subdivisions and factories.\n
[0m[1m	Meanwhile the peasant movement has remained in the streets, many of its\n
[0m[1m	leaders, now senior citizens, still pushing, even pathetically just so Congress\n
[0m[1m	would extend the life of CARPER two more years and Notice of Coverage could\n
[0m[1m	still be issued to hundreds of thousands of hectares of land left uncovered, including\n
[0m[1m	the 14,000 hectares of grabbed land (by Danding) in Bugsuk Island in Balabac,\n
[0m[1m[32m	Palawan.<o:[0m[1mp></o:p></span></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom:[0m[1m .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom:[0m[1m .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;">\n
[0m[1m[32m	<span style="font-family:[0m[1m &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">Far from its original vision, a\n
[0m[1m	government centerpiece program not very much unlike that which catapulted\n
[0m[1m	Taiwan, South Korea and Japan to industrialization and modernization, CARP did\n
[0m[1m	not get the Presidential leadership it badly needed (except, perhaps during\n
[0m[1m	Ramos). Some 4 million farmers who received land (some 7 million hectares\n
[0m[1m	reportedly distributed) remained un-attended with the necessary support\n
[0m[1m	services (credit, extension, market, etc.), mostly still living below poverty\n
[0m[1m[32m	line.<o:[0m[1mp></o:p></span></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom:[0m[1m .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom:[0m[1m .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;">\n
[0m[1m[32m	<span style="font-family:[0m[1m &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">Butch, as DBM Secretary, and with\n
[0m[1m	strong support from PNoy, could have the second chance to help ensure funding\n
[0m[1m	availability to support millions of agrarian reform beneficiaries achieve their\n
[0m[1m[32m	historic nation building role.<o:[0m[1mp></o:p></span></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom:[0m[1m .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom:[0m[1m .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;">\n
[0m[1m[32m	<span style="font-family:[0m[1m &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">We just hope and pray, he does not\n
[0m[1m	experience another awkward situation in the Cabinet and succumb the second\n
[0m[1m[32m	time...and resign.&nbsp;<o:[0m[1mp></o:p></span></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom:[0m[1m .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m	<br />\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom:[0m[1m .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;">\n
[0m[1m[32m	<span style="font-family:[0m[1m &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">We encourage him to stay put and stand\n
[0m[1m	his ground, and remain united with reform forces in government, and to continue\n
[0m[1m	to join the march of a people who has finally decided to take head-on the\n
[0m[1m	scourge of patronage politics. A new day is dawning...three Senators will soon\n
[0m[1m[32m	be in jail.&nbsp;<o:[0m[1mp></o:p></span></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div style='clear:[0m[1m both;'></div>\n
[0m[1m	</div>\n

[0m[1m	        \n
[0m[1m	<h2 class='date-header'><span>Friday, May 16, 2014</span></h2>\n
[0m[1m	\n
[0m[1m	          <div class="date-posts">\n
[0m[1m	        \n
[0m[1m	<div class='post-outer'>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http:[0m[1m//schema.org/BlogPosting'>\n
[0m[1m	<meta content='17476693' itemprop='blogId'/>\n
[0m[1m	<meta content='947306036162075388' itemprop='postId'/>\n
[0m[1m	<a name='947306036162075388'></a>\n
[0m[1m	<div class='post-header'>\n
[0m[1m	<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>\n
[0m[1m	</div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-947306036162075388' itemprop='description articleBody'>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom:[0m[1m .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;">\n
[0m[1m	<b>THE WOUNDED\n
[0m[1m[32m	PUBLIC SERVANT</b><o:[0m[1mp></o:p></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom:[0m[1m .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;">\n
[0m[1m	Corazon\n
[0m[1m[32m	Juliano Soliman<o:[0m[1mp></o:p></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	 [truncated]<span style="font-family:[0m[1m &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bi
[0m[1m	<br />\n
[0m[1m	Last April 27th,&nbsp;Sunday, the homily of Fr. Francis really struck me. &nbsp;He spoke about our hesitance to talk about our\n
[0m[1m	wounds and encouraged us to do so.... as Jesus did when he showed and invited\n
[0m[1m	the apostles to touch his wounds... It was not easy to listen as he shared and\n
[0m[1m	he spoke about his dilemma when he wrote a book about the son of a priest, that\n
[0m[1m	it takes courage and humility to talk about our wounds even with our family\n
[0m[1m	members and closest friends.<br />\n
[0m[1m	<br />\n
[0m[1m	It has taken me almost two week to write this reflection piece because I was\n
[0m[1m	afraid that it may be misinterpreted or even derided and twisted to allude\n
[0m[1m	meanings that are far from my own thoughts.&nbsp;\n
[0m[1m	I have been nudged every day since that homily to write, by my\n
[0m[1m	conscience.<br />\n
[0m[1m	<br />\n
[0m[1m	As public servants we live in a fish bowl.&nbsp;\n
[0m[1m	We cannot separate most of our public life from our private life, thus\n
[0m[1m	our family and friends are always affected by public perception -&nbsp;negative\n
[0m[1m	or positive feedback.<br />\n
[0m[1m	<br />\n
[0m[1m	I have known Butch Abad since the 1970's. &nbsp;Together with his wife Dina we were part of\n
[0m[1m	the movement for democracy. &nbsp;He was\n
[0m[1m	jailed together with Dina and their baby Julia in the late 70s because of their\n
[0m[1m	involvement in the anti-dictatorship movement. &nbsp;After temporary release he took up law while\n
[0m[1m	he continued to contribute to the effort of conscientization and mobilization\n
[0m[1m	of the Citizens for Democracy.<br />\n
[0m[1m	<br />\n
[0m[1m	Butch worked with Atty. Hector Soliman, my husband, to initiate and organize an\n
[0m[1m	alternative law practice - as mentored by Sen. Pepe Diokno - wherein people's\n
[0m[1m	organizations were assisted by lawyers who provided legal support during their\n
[0m[1m	struggle for their right to development.&nbsp;\n
[0m[1m	This blossomed and grew into the Alternative Law Groups we know today.<br />\n
[0m[1m	<br />\n
[0m[1m[32m	Butch entered the legislative arena as congressman and he initiated laws:[0m[1m\n
[0m[1m	supported legislation that institutionalized reforms such the agrarian reform\n
[0m[1m	law, and the people's participation&nbsp;bills. Those actions were consistent\n
[0m[1m	with the values and the principles we stood for. &nbsp;Again, as evidence of his commitment to social\n
[0m[1m	justice and truth, whenever faced with a cross road of actions that could\n
[0m[1m	compromise his principles and values, Butch always took the difficult path by\n
[0m[1m	following his conscience - he resigned as Secretary of Agrarian Reform during\n
[0m[1m	Pres. Cory 's administration - a very difficult decision because he loved Pres.\n
[0m[1m	Cory; he chose to leave the Arroyo administration when again truth was\n
[0m[1m	compromised and suffered the consequences of this action such as the\n
[0m[1m	marginalizing of their home province Batanes... Butch has stood for his\n
[0m[1m	principles by taking the difficult path instead of the easy path of\n
[0m[1m	compromising principles.<br />\n
[0m[1m	<br />\n
[0m[1m	When he took up the challenge of being DBM secretary to manage the coffers of\n
[0m[1m	the government, Butch opened up the systems, information and the processes so\n
[0m[1m	that our citizens could track budgets and expenditures, participate in the\n
[0m[1m	budget process and ensure that the funds are spent in a judicious and\n
[0m[1m	responsive manner.<br />\n
[0m[1m	<br />\n
[0m[1m	And yet today he is maligned as the person who taught Napoles the tricks about stealing\n
[0m[1m	via NGOs... I am sure it hurts him, the wounds cut deep and wide... and yet he\n
[0m[1m	will not speak about his wounds. &nbsp;He\n
[0m[1m	continues to do his work, silently bearing the pain even as he tries to show\n
[0m[1m	the public that he is a person of integrity and principle.<br />\n
[0m[1m	<br />\n
[0m[1m	Most of us in public service carry the same wounds.&nbsp; Maybe not as big and deep as those suffered\n
[0m[1m	by Butch, but we all feel that there are many times that we are sacrificial\n
[0m[1m	lambs on the altar of political ambitions of those who may not necessarily be\n
[0m[1m	acting on behalf the common and highest good.<br />\n
[0m[1m	<br />\n
[0m[1m	This reflection piece is for all of us who are wounded public servants.&nbsp; It is good to talk about our wounds and let\n
[0m[1m	our loved ones,&nbsp;family and friends touch them. Their loving touch provides\n
[0m[1m	the gentle healing we need to carry on our mahusay, matapat and magiliw na\n
[0m[1m	paglilingkod sa sambayanan. -- END</span>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div style='clear:[0m[1m both;'></div>\n
[0m[1m	</div>\n

[0m[1m	<h2 class='date-header'><span>Tuesday, May 13, 2014</span></h2>\n
[0m[1m	\n
[0m[1m	          <div class="date-posts">\n
[0m[1m	        \n
[0m[1m	<div class='post-outer'>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http:[0m[1m//schema.org/BlogPosting'>\n
[0m[1m	<meta content='17476693' itemprop='blogId'/>\n
[0m[1m	<meta content='7809178010627845328' itemprop='postId'/>\n
[0m[1m	<a name='7809178010627845328'></a>\n
[0m[1m	<div class='post-header'>\n
[0m[1m	<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>\n

[0m[1m	<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-7809178010627845328' itemprop='description articleBody'>\n
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	<b><u>STATEMENT BY SEC. FLORENCIO B. ABAD ON THE SUPPOSED\n
[0m[1m[32m	NAPOLES LISTS</u></b><o:[0m[1mp></o:p></div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	"I have never dealt with Janet Lim Napoles or any of\n
[0m[1m[32m	her fake NGOs in any way throughout my career in public service:[0m[1m either as\n
[0m[1m	representative of Batanes, as Budget and Management Secretary, or as an\n
[0m[1m	official of any other public office that has been entrusted to me. I have spent\n
[0m[1m	my professional life&#8212;inside government and in civil society&#8212;working to improve\n
[0m[1m[32m	the lives of ordinary Filipinos by pushing for reforms in public governance.<o:[0m[1mp></o:p></div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	&#8220;Moreover, all projects I sponsored under the Priority\n
[0m[1m	Development Assistance Fund (PDAF) when I was a legislator are above board&#8212;none\n
[0m[1m	have been coursed through any fake NGO. Unlike other personalities dragged into\n
[0m[1m	the PDAF Scam of 2007-2009, who have been implicated by evidence and testimony\n
[0m[1m	by whistleblowers, nothing credible has been brought against me &#8211; but rather,\n
[0m[1m[32m	unfounded allegations and malicious name-calling.<o:[0m[1mp></o:p></div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	&#8220;I find it amusing, if not outright revolting, that I am\n
[0m[1m	once again in the crosshairs of those who want the Aquino Administration to\n
[0m[1m	fall.&nbsp;<i>Matagal ko nang tanggap na idadawit ako kung saan-saan gawa ng\n
[0m[1m	aming trabaho sa DBM bilang tagapangalaga ng kaban ng bayan at tagasulong ng\n
[0m[1m	reporma sa pamahalaan&#8212;lalo na&#8217;t pinaiigting ngayon ng Administrasyong Aquino\n
[0m[1m	ang Daang Matuwid</i>.&nbsp;<i>Habang lumalapit ang 2016, tiyak na marami pang\n
[0m[1m	lalabas na absurdong alegasyon. Tiwala akong masasala ng publiko ang mga\n
[0m[1m[32m	kuwentong imbento lang, at maninindigan sila para sa katotohanan</i>."<o:[0m[1mp></o:p></div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	"Until the public sees the true affidavit of Janet Lim\n
[0m[1m	Napoles, and until hard evidence supports the statements in this affidavit,\n
[0m[1m	everything is speculation, if not total fabrication, at this point. I ask the\n
[0m[1m	public not to immediately believe these allegations, but to weigh the only\n
[0m[1m[32m	thing that matters in the end:[0m[1m the evidence. I urge the Department of Justice\n
[0m[1m	and the Ombudsman to continue their investigation, follow the evidence wherever\n
[0m[1m[32m	it may lead them, and take appropriate action on behalf of the people.&#8221;<o:[0m[1mp></o:p></div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	<i><u>For inquiries, further questions and requests for\n
[0m[1m[32m	interview, please contact:[0m[1m</u></i><o:p></o:p></div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m[32m	<b>OSEC-Public Information Unit&nbsp;</b><o:[0m[1mp></o:p></div>\n

[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n

[0m[1m[32m	 [truncated]And as history and some unassailable sources avow, this would not be the first time Enrile &#8220;shot himself&#8217;. In Juan Ponce Enrile:[0m[1m A Memoir, and bio-documentary &#8220;Johnny&#8221; that aired in ABS-CBN--- he recant
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n

[0m[1m	 [truncated]&#8220;This accusation is ridiculous and preposterous. What would I have faked my ambush for?&#8221; By that time martial law was already an &#8220;irreversible fact&#8221; since documents had been signed and the military oper
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	&#8220;I honestly did not know why Marcos suddenly decided to cite my ambush in justifying the declaration of martial law when he made his public statement on September 23. There was absolutely no need for it.&#8221;</div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	 [truncated]Did he expect national amnesia to afflict Filipinos who know the truth? Are we expected to forget the press conference that he and and then Lt. Gen. Fidel Ramos called on Feb 22,1986 in the Ministry of National Defense when th
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	 [truncated]This fact is further documented in various books written by foreign journalists who covered those perilous years. Time correspondent Sandra Burton, wrote in her book Impossible Dream(1989), &#8220;Seasoned observers believed f
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	 [truncated]Raymond Bonner of the New York Times interviewed Enrile twice in 1985. In his book Waltzing with a Dictator(1988) he wrote, &#8220;He was emphatic that the attack on him had not been staged, but in February 1986, after he had 
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	 [truncated]Pulitzer Prize-winning journalist Katherine Ellison also wrote in her 1988 book, Imelda,&#8220;(Enrile) revealed that he had narrowly escaped injury in a spectacular ambush of his car&#8212;an event he conceded in 1986 had bee
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	 [truncated]In his attempt to leave an acceptable legacy for posterity and bequeath a Senate seat for junior, the nonagenarian is sanitizing his recollections instead of asking for absolution. Stem cell therapy can deter dementia but it c
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	 [truncated]And now the gullible electorate is being enticed to continue Enrile&#8217;s political dominion through the son, Jack. By his own narrative, Junior was not close to his father in his younger days. He recalled that as a child, h
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	 [truncated]Jack has his own intrigues to expunge. On December 30,1981, actor Alfie Anido, then the boyfriend of his sister Katrina was found dead. The tale turns murky but Jack was seenin the Anidos&#8217; Bel-Air residence inside the ro
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	 [truncated]In his book, the elder Enrile said there was no doubt that Jack&#8217;s supposed role was the handiwork of Fabian Ver. &#8220;No doubt, the only purpose of those who spread that false rumor was to besmirch my family and destro
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	 [truncated]In the documentary, the young Enrile recalled responding to his sister&#8217;s call for help. He said he joined his father&#8217;s chief security aide, Gringo Honasan in Bel-Air.That&#8217;s when he found Anido dead from a gun
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	 [truncated]Another misdeed associated with father-and-son is the alleged rampant car smuggling in Port Irene. In 1995, the Cagayan Export Zone Authority (CEZA) was established through Republic Act 7922, authored by Cagayan native JPE. Am
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	 [truncated]The flourishing buy-and-sell of secondhand cars in Port Irene &nbsp;prodded the American Chamber of Commerce to submit a letter of concern to then Finance Secretary Margarito Teves. Despite EO156 issued in 2008, which prohibit
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	There&#8217;s a father-and-son story that comes to mind---</div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m[32m	A father overheard his son pray:[0m[1m Dear God, make me the man my Dad is. Later, the father prayed: Dear God, Make me the man my son wants me to be.</div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m[32m	We are being wooed to perpetuate the forty-years-running Enrile saga. Every night we should pray:[0m[1m Dear God, Make all who want our vote, be the men we want them to be.</div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class="MsoNormal">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n

[0m[1m	<h2 class='date-header'><span>Friday, October 12, 2012</span></h2>\n
[0m[1m	\n
[0m[1m	          <div class="date-posts">\n
[0m[1m	        \n
[0m[1m	<div class='post-outer'>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http:[0m[1m//schema.org/BlogPosting'>\n
[0m[1m	<meta content='17476693' itemprop='blogId'/>\n
[0m[1m	<meta content='6778880337483741360' itemprop='postId'/>\n
[0m[1m	<a name='6778880337483741360'></a>\n
[0m[1m	<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<a href='http:[0m[1m//blacknwhitemovement.blogspot.com/2012/10/leah-navarro-does-not-represent-urban.html'>LEAH NAVARRO DOES NOT REPRESENT THE URBAN POOR</a>\n
[0m[1m	</h3>\n
[0m[1m	<div class='post-header'>\n
[0m[1m	<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>\n
[0m[1m	</div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-6778880337483741360' itemprop='description articleBody'>\n
[0m[1m	<br />\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m	</div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m	</div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m[32m	<span style="font-family:[0m[1m Arial, sans-serif; line-height: 115%;">First, there was KontraDaya.\n
[0m[1m	Now, it&#8217;s Anakbayan. Both are part of the ultra-leftist coalition of Bayan and\n
[0m[1m	the Makabayan Coalition. These groups have waged an all-out campaign to\n
[0m[1m	discredit all Party List aspirants not aligned with their Maoist agenda &#8211;\n
[0m[1m[32m	including Black and White.<o:[0m[1mp></o:p></span></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m[32m	<span style="font-family:[0m[1m Arial, sans-serif; line-height: 115%;">Unfortunately, people buy\n
[0m[1m[32m	into their propaganda without bothering to check the facts.<o:[0m[1mp></o:p></span></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m[32m	<span style="font-family:[0m[1m Arial, sans-serif; line-height: 115%;">Before its creation, the\n
[0m[1m	conveners and members of the Black and White Movement were veteran advocates of\n
[0m[1m	various social causes. Undeniably, our nominees do indeed stand for their\n
[0m[1m[32m	sectors.<o:[0m[1mp></o:p></span></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m[32m	<span style="font-family:[0m[1m Arial, sans-serif; line-height: 115%;">They say Leah Navarro cannot\n
[0m[1m	possibly represent the urban poor. In our application for accreditation, we\n
[0m[1m	never said she did. She represents <b><i>women</i></b> &#8211; a sector specifically\n
[0m[1m	defined by the Party List Law as marginalized and under represented. And, why\n
[0m[1m	not? Leah has supported women&#8217;s rights causes even before joining Black and\n
[0m[1m	White. She is an advocate for responsible parenthood and has actively opposed\n
[0m[1m	violence against women. She has represented Black and White at events and\n
[0m[1m	projects supportive of various women&#8217;s causes alongside fellow conveners Karen\n
[0m[1m[32m	Tanada and Beth Yang.<o:[0m[1mp></o:p></span></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m[32m	<span style="font-family:[0m[1m Arial, sans-serif; line-height: 115%;">We wonder why they never mention\n
[0m[1m[32m	our second and third nominees because, like Leah, they represent their sectors.<o:[0m[1mp></o:p></span></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m[32m	<span style="font-family:[0m[1m Arial, sans-serif; line-height: 115%;">Our second nominee is Marco\n
[0m[1m	Cabrera &#8211; a leader of our Black and White Youth chapter. This segment of the\n
[0m[1m	Black and White organization started in 2009 in the Camanava area where it has\n
[0m[1m	been actively involved in engaging the youth via community service projects and\n
[0m[1m	involvement in political issues, focusing on truth, accountability and good\n
[0m[1m	governance. Again, the youth is one sector specifically defined by the Party\n
[0m[1m[32m	List Law as marginalized.<o:[0m[1mp></o:p></span></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m[32m	<span style="font-family:[0m[1m Arial, sans-serif; line-height: 115%;">Our third nominee is Ka Jose\n
[0m[1m	Morales &#8211; a leader of our Black and White Katipunan &#8211; an urban poor group based\n
[0m[1m	in the Taytay-Antipolo area, which has been part of Black and White since its\n
[0m[1m	inception in 2005. A tireless campaigner for the rights of our impoverished, Ka\n
[0m[1m	Jose is a convener of AKKMA (Aksyon sa Kalamidad at Klima), Ugnayang Lakas ng\n
[0m[1m	mga Apektadong Pamilya sa Baybaying Ilog Pasig (ULAP) and the Urban Poor\n
[0m[1m[32m	Alliance (UPALL). Definitely, the urban poor are marginalized.<o:[0m[1mp></o:p></span></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m[32m	<span style="font-family:[0m[1m Arial, sans-serif; line-height: 115%;">While it is true that some\n
[0m[1m	of our conveners are now in the Executive branch of government, it does not\n
[0m[1m	change the fact that Black and White has been actively engaged in advancing the\n
[0m[1m	causes of sectors considered as marginalized &#8211; women, youth, and urban poor. If\n
[0m[1m	given the opportunity, we are committed to protect and advance our multi-sector\n
[0m[1m[32m	interests through responsive legislation.<o:[0m[1mp></o:p></span></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m[32m	<span style="font-family:[0m[1m Arial, sans-serif; line-height: 115%;">We appeal to everyone to\n
[0m[1m	check the facts before buying into these groups&#8217; Maoist-communist propaganda.\n
[0m[1m	Let us not leave the Party List system in the hands of leftist extremists that\n
[0m[1m[32m	are hell bent on blocking the daan na matuwid.<a href="" name="_GoBack"></a> -- END<span style="font-size:[0m[1m x-small;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n
[0m[1m	<br />\n
[0m[1m	<br />\n

[0m[1m	<div class='post-outer'>\n

[0m[1m	<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<a href='http:[0m[1m//blacknwhitemovement.blogspot.com/2012/09/the-party-list-system-is-not-exclusive.html'>THE PARTY LIST SYSTEM IS NOT EXCLUSIVE TO LEFTISTS</a>\n
[0m[1m	</h3>\n
[0m[1m	<div class='post-header'>\n
[0m[1m	<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>\n
[0m[1m	</div>\n
[0m[1m	<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-7921431548464188412' itemprop='description articleBody'>\n
[0m[1m	<br />\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m[32m	<span style="font-size:[0m[1m 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">BnW Media Press Release</span></span></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m[32m	<span style="font-size:[0m[1m 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">29 September 2012</span></span></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m[32m	<span style="font-size:[0m[1m 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><br /></span></span></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m[32m	<span style="font-size:[0m[1m 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">A leftist, anti-Aquino administration group purporting to be\n
[0m[1m	a non-partisan citizen&#8217;s group named Kontra Daya has called on the Black and\n
[0m[1m	White Movement to withdraw its application for accreditation as a Regional\n
[0m[1m	Political Party participating in the 2013 Party List election. It claims our\n
[0m[1m[32m	close alliance with President Aquino makes a mockery of the Party List system.<o:[0m[1mp></o:p></span></span></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m[32m	<span style="font-size:[0m[1m 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">To Kontra Daya, which is led by Fr. Joe Dizon, a close\n
[0m[1m	associate of the Bayan coalition and Bayan Muna Party List, we have one simple\n
[0m[1m[32m	question:[0m[1m With due respect to Sen. Manny Villar (and the NP, now in coalition\n
[0m[1m	with the LP for the upcoming elections), whom Bayan allies supported in the\n
[0m[1m	2010 presidential election, if he had won &#8211; would Bayan Muna withdraw its\n
[0m[1m[32m	participation in the 2013 Party List election?<o:[0m[1mp></o:p></span></span></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m[32m	<span style="font-size:[0m[1m 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">For the record, ever since our inception in 2005, the Black\n
[0m[1m	and White Movement has always worked with the urban poor sector. They were with\n
[0m[1m	us in our mass actions against the excesses of the GMA regime. In fact, the\n
[0m[1m	lead convener of Black and White Katipunan (our Urban Poor cluster), Ka Jose\n
[0m[1m[32m	Morales, is our third nominee.<o:[0m[1mp></o:p></span></span></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m[32m	<span style="font-size:[0m[1m 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">For the record, we also have a very active and passionate\n
[0m[1m	youth group &#8211; the Black and White Youth Movement and one of its leaders, Marco\n
[0m[1m[32m	Cabrera, is our second nominee.<o:[0m[1mp></o:p></span></span></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m[32m	<span style="font-size:[0m[1m 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">For the record, many of our conveners &#8211; Karen Tanada, Elizabeth\n
[0m[1m	Yang, and Leah Navarro are prominent advocates of women&#8217;s rights and\n
[0m[1m	issues.&nbsp; We have chosen Leah Navarro &#8211;\n
[0m[1m	our first nominee, to represent the women&#8217;s sector. Her current appointment as\n
[0m[1m	MTRCB board member ends on 30 September 2012 and does not conflict with this\n
[0m[1m[32m	advocacy. She cannot be reappointed when our accreditation is approved.<o:[0m[1mp></o:p></span></span></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m[32m	<span style="font-size:[0m[1m 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">These sectors &#8211; women, youth, and urban poor - are\n
[0m[1m[32m	 [truncated]specifically identified by the&nbsp;</span></span><b style="font-family:[0m[1m Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 13px; line-height: 14px;"><a href="http://www.chanrobles.com/republicactno7941.htm#.UGgBt5jMio0" target="_blank"
[0m[1m	requirements for a Regional Political Party (NCR) participating in the Party\n
[0m[1m	List system. All of our nominees belong to the sectors being represented. And\n
[0m[1m	none of them are former politicians. None of them are associated with any\n
[0m[1m	business interest or political clan.</span></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m[32m	<span style="font-size:[0m[1m 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">WE ARE QUALIFIED TO PARTICIPATE IN THE PARTY LIST\n
[0m[1m	ELECTION.&nbsp; And if elected, we are\n
[0m[1m	committed to sponsor and support legislation that will protect and advance the\n
[0m[1m[32m	interests of the sectors we represent.<o:[0m[1mp></o:p></span></span></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height:[0m[1m 115%;">\n
[0m[1m	<br /></div>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<span style="font-size:[0m[1m 10pt;"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Contrary to what Kontra Daya thinks, you do not\n
[0m[1m	have to be a leftist to qualify in the Party List system and fight for the\n
[0m[1m	marginalized. - END</span></span>\n
[0m[1m[32m	<div style='clear:[0m[1m both;'></div>\n
